    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
      var hash = window.decodeURI(location.hash.replace('#', ''))
      if (hash !== '') {
        var element = document.getElementById(hash)
        if (element) {
          var scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop
          var clientTop = document.documentElement.clientTop || document.body.clientTop || 0
          var offset = element.getBoundingClientRect().top + scrollTop - clientTop
          // Wait for the browser to finish rendering before scrolling.
          setTimeout((function() {
            window.scrollTo(0, offset - 0)
          }), 0)
        }

--> </a></li><li><a href="/team/">Team<!-- --> </a></li><li><a href="https://blog.celestia.org" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer">Blog</a></li></ul></nav><div class="clear"></div></div></header><div class="index-page"><main><section class="hero-section"><div class="container"><h1>The first modular blockchain network</h1><div class="text">Celestia is a modular consensus and data network, built to enable anyone to easily deploy their own blockchain with minimal overhead.</div><a class="button button-simple" href="/#roadmap">See the roadmap</a><a class="button button-white" href="/#join-the-community">Join the community</a></div></section><div class="container"><h2 class="with-decor">Advantages</h2><section class="advantages-section"><div class="row"><div class="col col-12 col-lg-6 pe-md-5"><div class="advantage mb-5 pb-lg-5 pt-lg-4"><div class="row"><div class="col col-12 col-sm-4 pe-sm-3"><div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-sm-8 ps-sm-3"><div class="title">Deploy a blockchain as easily as a smart contract</div><div class="text">Celestia provides consensus and security on-demand, enabling anyone to deploy a blockchain without the overhead of bootstrapping a new consensus network.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-lg-6 pe-md-5"><div class="advantage mb-5 pb-lg-5 pt-lg-4"><div class="row"><div class="col col-12 col-sm-4 pe-sm-3"><div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-sm-8 ps-sm-3"><div class="title">Scaling made simple with data availability sampling</div><div class="text">Because Celestia does not validate transactions, its throughput is not bottlenecked by state execution like traditional blockchains. Thanks to a property of data availability sampling, Celestias throughput scales with the number of users.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-lg-6 pe-md-5"><div class="advantage mb-5 pb-lg-5 pt-lg-4"><div class="row"><div class="col col-12 col-sm-4 pe-sm-3"><div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-sm-8 ps-sm-3"><div class="title">Secure interoperability for all Celestia chains</div><div class="text">Blockchains built on top of Celestia do not rely on honest majority assumptions for state validity, meaning that they can interoperate with the highest security standards.</div></div></div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-lg-6 pe-md-5"><div class="advantage mb-5 pb-lg-5 pt-lg-4"><div class="row"><div class="col col-12 col-sm-4 pe-sm-3"><div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-sm-8 ps-sm-3"><div class="title">Choose your own execution environment</div><div class="text">Since Celestia does not impose any execution logic, developers are free to define their own execution environments. Celestia will support all flavors of rollups, but we are initially focused on the EVM and Cosmos SDK.</div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="row justify-content-center"><div class="col-auto"><a class="button button-simple" href="/technology/">Learn more</a></div></div></section><section class="cards-section"><h2 class="with-decor pb-2">How it works</h2><div class="subtitle">Celestia is a minimal blockchain that only orders and publishes transactions and does not execute them. By decoupling the consensus and application execution layers, Celestia modularizes the blockchain technology stack and unlocks new possibilities for decentralized application builders.</div><div class="row mt-5"><div class="col col-12 col-lg-6 pe-lg-4"><div class="card"><div class="image-container"><div class=" gatsby-image-wrapper" style="position:relative;overflow:hidden"><div class="title">Traditional monolithic architecture</div><div class="text"><ul><li>Developers can only use programming languages supported by chain's execution environment</li><li>All applications run on the same process (the world computer model), with shared gas resources</li><li>Smart contracts cannot be updated without a hard fork</li></ul></div></div></div></div><div class="col col-12 col-lg-6 class="title">Celestia-enabled modular architecture</div><div class="text"><ul><li>Developers can effortlessly define their own virtual execution environments; similar to virtual machines</li><li>Each application gets its own sovereign execution space, while inheriting the security of Celestia's consensus</li><li>Applications can be updated without main chain hard forks</li></ul></div></div></div></div></div><div class="row justify-content-center pt-5"><div class="col-auto"><div class="button button-simple button-internal" role="button" tabindex="0"
